info:Stayed in May 2024

info:5 Reviews
rating:2.5
posted:Posted May 29, 2024
msg:I have never stayed in a hotel with such poor hygiene! Is there no training for housekeeping? Does the supervisor not check?
When booking, there were three five-star hotels around. I thought that Shangri-La had the highest price, so how bad could it be? Besides, the Ctrip rating was quite high, so I booked it. What a result! I understand that the facilities and decoration style of old hotels may be weak, and I am prepared, so I saw that the weak three-no brand mini hair dryer in the room was not surprised, but the hygiene situation was really beyond my expectation!
After entering, the first thing I saw on the carpet was a large black stain that was really hard to ignore. It was so bright black that it had never been cleaned! The sofa was really rubbed with oil and shiny, and it was not easy to insist on being used even if it was about to break. Good! I comforted myself that the carpet cleaning of the old hotel may also need to be cleaned uniformly at a fixed time...
But! Is it too much to have such obvious sticky marks on the sofa table! It can be seen that the room cleaning has not been wiped at all! As for the dust in various corners, it must have been accumulated for who knows how long, and the conditioner was opened... I can choose to ignore these if I don't touch them... Finally, I really didn't dare to look at the bedding, so I put on disposable sheets when I came up, fearing that I would feel more upset after seeing them...
I really saw a lot of good reviews when I booked, I didn't expect the hygiene to be so bad! But I found that not only the guest rooms, but also the boxes of disinfectants in the elevator were covered with a layer of dust... It's really hard to rate...
The only good thing to say is that the uncles and brothers in the concierge are all cute and enthusiastic, I only want to give them stars.

The process that usually takes a few minutes actually took about twelve minutes, and the price reported on Ctrip.com was calculated a few more dollars, and the staff did not understand what was going on. Secondly, there is no elevator in the underground garage to reach the hotel lobby. Every time you go to the garage to pick up the car, you have to climb several stairs. The parking outside the lobby is chaotic. Because the lobby door is close to the entrance and exit of the underground garage, the staff cannot clear the waiting vehicles in the first time, which causes the lobby door to be a mess. Secondly, the layout of the restaurant environment in the morning and evening is too small, and the tables and chairs are placed too closely. When the guests pick up the food, they encounter the vehicles that the staff pushes the tableware. They are almost always in close contact with the guests who pick up the food, which easily makes the guests' clothes dirty. Finally, when the guests eat, due to the imperfect and meticulous handover of the front desk and restaurant staff, there is always a long queue when the guests eat. The only thing worth praising is the room attendant, who is responsive to requests. The others are speechless and their hearts are completely cold, so this hotel will not be checked in again before it is thoroughly improved.
